types = {
	#TODO: отполировать шансы успехов для налетов
	#TODO: вписывать в результат налета полученый урон мостом(?)
	#Киевская ГЭС (Киев)
	strikes_on_bridges_KYIV_HYDRA_STRAIT_rc = {
		days_to_prepare = 1
		days_re_enable = 0
		category = on_bridge_strikes
		command_power = 0
		 ai_will_do = {
		 	base = 1.0
		 	modifier = {
		 		factor = 5.0
		 		date > 2022.3.1
		 	}
		 	modifier = {
		 		factor = 0.2
		 		date < 2022.3.1
		 	}
		 }
		allowed = {
			has_dlc = "Gotterdammerung"
		}
		visible = {
		}
		show_target = {
			NOT = { is_in_faction_with = FROM }
			has_war_with = FROM
		}
		available = {
			has_war_with = FROM
		}
		target_type = {
			province = 15949
		}
		target_icon = GFX_other_target_icon
		launch_sound = raid_launch_air
		arrow = {
			type = air
		}
		unit_model = {
		}
		unit_requirements = {
			equipment = {
				type = { ukr_light_guided_missile_equipment ukr_sea_guided_missile_equipment nto_light_guided_missile_equipment nto_medium_guided_missile_equipment nto_sea_guided_missile_equipment rus_light_guided_missile_equipment rus_medium_guided_missile_equipment }
				amount = { min = 4 }
			}
		}
		additional_equipment = {
		}
		starting_point = {
			types = {
				rocket_site
			}
		}
		success_factors = {
			success = {
				base = 0.4
				air_agility = {
					reference = 20
					weight = 0.1
					start_weight = -0.5
				}
				reliability = {
					reference = 1
					weight = 0.1
					start_weight = -0.1
				}
				air_superiority = {
					reference = 1
					weight = 0.3
					start_weight = -0.100
				}

				anti_air = {
					reference = 1
					weight = -0.3
				}
				radar = {
					reference = 0
					weight = -0.2
				}
				interception = {
					reference = 5 
					weight = -0.2
				}
				intel = {
					weight = 0.1
					reference = 100
				}
			}
			disaster = {
				base = 0.2
			}
			critical = {
				base = 0.05
			}
		}
		success_levels = {
			failure = {
				victim_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = {
						missle_strike_dmg = 0
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = bridges_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?missle_strike_dmg]
					}
				}
				actor_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 4 }
					
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = plane_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?raid_planes_lost]
					}

					hidden_effect = {
						raid_damage_units = {
							plane_loss = raid_planes_lost
							ratio = no
						}
					}
				}
			}
			limited_success = {
				victim_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = {
						missle_strike_dmg = 10
					}
					subtract_from_variable = {
						global.dnipro_obj_current_hp^0 = missle_strike_dmg
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = bridges_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?missle_strike_dmg]
					}
				}
				actor_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lostt = 4 }
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 1 }

					var:target_state = {
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.aa_defense = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@anti_air_building }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.radar_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@radar_station }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.rocket_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@rocket_site }
					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { radar_mult = 0.5 }
					multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = radar_mult }
					multiply_temp_variable = { rocket_mult = radar_mult }

					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { check_variable = { rocket_mult = 0 } }
						}
						multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { aa_defense = 0 }
							}
							add_to_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }
						}
					}

					multiply_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = aa_defense integer = yes }

					clamp_temp_variable = {
						var = raid_planes_lost
						min = 0
					}

					round_temp_variable = raid_planes_lost

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost > 3 } 
						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 3 } 
					}

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 0 } 
						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 2 } 
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = plane_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?raid_planes_lost]
					}

					hidden_effect = {
						raid_damage_units = {
							plane_loss = raid_planes_lostt
							ratio = no
						}
					}
				}
			}
			success = {
				victim_effects = {
					set_temp_variable_to_random = {
						var = missle_strike_dmg
						min = 10
						max = 25
						integer = yes
					}
					subtract_from_variable = {
						global.dnipro_obj_current_hp^0 = missle_strike_dmg
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = bridges_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?missle_strike_dmg]
					}
				}
				actor_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lostt = 4 }
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 1 }

					var:target_state = {
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.aa_defense = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@anti_air_building }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.radar_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@radar_station }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.rocket_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@rocket_site }
					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { radar_mult = 0.5 }
					multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = radar_mult }
					multiply_temp_variable = { rocket_mult = radar_mult }

					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { check_variable = { rocket_mult = 0 } }
						}
						multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { aa_defense = 0 }
							}
							add_to_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }
						}
					}

					multiply_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = aa_defense integer = yes }

					clamp_temp_variable = {
						var = raid_planes_lost
						min = 0
					}

					round_temp_variable = raid_planes_lost

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost > 3 } 
						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 3 } 
					}

					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = plane_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?raid_planes_lost]
					}

					hidden_effect = {
						raid_damage_units = {
							plane_loss = raid_planes_lostt
							ratio = no
						}
					}
				}
			}
			critical_success = {
				victim_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = {
						missle_strike_dmg = 40
					}
					subtract_from_variable = {
						global.dnipro_obj_current_hp^0 = missle_strike_dmg
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = bridges_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?missle_strike_dmg]
					}
				}
				actor_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lostt = 4 }
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 0 }

					var:target_state = {
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.aa_defense = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@anti_air_building }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.radar_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@radar_station }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.rocket_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@rocket_site }
					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { radar_mult = 0.5 }

					multiply_temp_variable = { rocket_mult = radar_mult }

						limit = {
							NOT = { check_variable = { rocket_mult = 0 } }
						}
						multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { aa_defense = 0 }
							}
							add_to_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }
						}
					}

					multiply_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = aa_defense integer = yes }

					clamp_temp_variable = {
						var = raid_planes_lost
						min = 0
					}

					round_temp_variable = raid_planes_lost

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost > 2 } 
						}

					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 1 }

					var:target_state = {
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.aa_defense = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@anti_air_building }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.radar_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@radar_station }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.rocket_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@rocket_site }
					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { radar_mult = 0.5 }
					multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = radar_mult }
					multiply_temp_variable = { rocket_mult = radar_mult }

					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { check_variable = { rocket_mult = 0 } }
						}
						multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { aa_defense = 0 }
							}
							add_to_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }
						}
					}

					multiply_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = aa_defense integer = yes }

					clamp_temp_variable = {
						var = raid_planes_lost
						min = 0
					}

					round_temp_variable = raid_planes_lost

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost > 12 } 
						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 10 } 
					}

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 0 } 
						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 4 } 
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = plane_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?raid_planes_lost]
					}

					hidden_effect = {
						raid_damage_units = {
							plane_loss = raid_planes_lostt
							ratio = no
						}
					}
				}
				
			}
			success = {
				victim_effects = {
					set_temp_variable_to_random = {
						var = missle_strike_dmg
						min = 20
						max = 40
						integer = yes
					}
					subtract_from_variable = {
						global.dnipro_obj_current_hp^0 = missle_strike_dmg
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = bridges_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?missle_strike_dmg]
					}
				}
				actor_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lostt = 12 }
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 1 }

					var:target_state = {
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.aa_defense = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@anti_air_building }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.radar_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@radar_station }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.rocket_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@rocket_site }
					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { radar_mult = 0.5 }
					multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = radar_mult }
					multiply_temp_variable = { rocket_mult = radar_mult }

					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { check_variable = { rocket_mult = 0 } }
						}
						multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { aa_defense = 0 }
							}
							add_to_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }
						}
					}

					multiply_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = aa_defense integer = yes }

					clamp_temp_variable = {
						var = raid_planes_lost
						min = 0
					}

					round_temp_variable = raid_planes_lost

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost > 10 } 
						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 8 } 
					}

					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = plane_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?raid_planes_lost]
					}

					hidden_effect = {
						raid_damage_units = {
							plane_loss = raid_planes_lostt
							ratio = no
						}
					}
				}
				
			}
			critical_success = {
				victim_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = {
						missle_strike_dmg = 50
					}
					subtract_from_variable = {
						global.dnipro_obj_current_hp^0 = missle_strike_dmg
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = bridges_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?missle_strike_dmg]
					}
				}
				actor_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lostt = 12 }
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 1 }

					var:target_state = {
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.aa_defense = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@anti_air_building }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.radar_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@radar_station }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.rocket_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@rocket_site }
					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { radar_mult = 0.5 }
					multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = radar_mult }
					multiply_temp_variable = { rocket_mult = radar_mult }

					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { check_variable = { rocket_mult = 0 } }
						}
						multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { aa_defense = 0 }
							}
							add_to_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }
						}
					}

					multiply_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = aa_defense integer = yes }

					clamp_temp_variable = {

						min = 0

						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 3 } 
					}

					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = plane_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?raid_planes_lost]
					}

					hidden_effect = {
						raid_damage_units = {
							plane_loss = raid_planes_lostt
							ratio = no
						}
					}
				}
				
			}
			critical_success = {
				victim_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = {
						missle_strike_dmg = 100
					}
					subtract_from_variable = {
						global.dnipro_obj_current_hp^0 = missle_strike_dmg
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = bridges_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?missle_strike_dmg]
					}
				}
				actor_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lostt = 4 }
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 0 }

					var:target_state = {
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.aa_defense = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@anti_air_building }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.radar_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@radar_station }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.rocket_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@rocket_site }
					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { radar_mult = 0.5 }
					multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = radar_mult }
					multiply_temp_variable = { rocket_mult = radar_mult }

					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { check_variable = { rocket_mult = 0 } }
						}
						multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { aa_defense = 0 }
							}
							add_to_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }
						}
					}

					multiply_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = aa_defense integer = yes }

					clamp_temp_variable = {
						var = raid_planes_lost
						min = 0
					}

					round_temp_variable = raid_planes_lost

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost > 2 } 
						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 2 } 
					}

					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = plane_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?raid_planes_lost]
					}

					hidden_effect = {
						raid_damage_units = {
							plane_loss = raid_planes_lostt
							ratio = no
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		}
		unit_requirements = {
			equipment = {
				type = { ballistic_missile_equipment rus_heavy_guided_missile_equipment }
				amount = { min = 4 }
			}
		}
		additional_equipment = {
		}
		starting_point = {
			types = {
				rocket_site
			}
		}
		success_factors = {
			success = {
				base = 0.4
				air_agility = {
					reference = 20
					weight = 0.1
					start_weight = -0.5
				}
				reliability = {
					reference = 1
					weight = 0.1
					start_weight = -0.1
				}
				air_superiority = {
					reference = 1
					weight = 0.3
					start_weight = -0.100
				}

				anti_air = {
					reference = 1
					weight = -0.3
				}

					reference = 0
					weight = -0.2

					reference = 5 
					weight = -0.2

					weight = 0.1

				base = 0.2
			}

				base = 0.05
			}
		}
		success_levels = {
			failure = {
				victim_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = {
						missle_strike_dmg = 0
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = bridges_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?missle_strike_dmg]
					}
				}
				actor_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 4 }
					
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = plane_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?raid_planes_lost]
					}

					hidden_effect = {
						raid_damage_units = {
							plane_loss = raid_planes_lost
							ratio = no
						}
					}
				}
			}
			limited_success = {
				victim_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = {
						missle_strike_dmg = 40
					}
					subtract_from_variable = {
						global.dnipro_obj_current_hp^10 = missle_strike_dmg
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = bridges_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?missle_strike_dmg]
					}
				}
				actor_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lostt = 4 }
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 1 }

					var:target_state = {
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.aa_defense = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@anti_air_building }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.radar_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@radar_station }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.rocket_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@rocket_site }
					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { radar_mult = 0.5 }
					multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = radar_mult }
					multiply_temp_variable = { rocket_mult = radar_mult }

					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { check_variable = { rocket_mult = 0 } }
						}
						multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { aa_defense = 0 }
							}
							add_to_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }
						}
					}

					multiply_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = aa_defense integer = yes }

					clamp_temp_variable = {
						var = raid_planes_lost
						min = 0
					}

					round_temp_variable = raid_planes_lost

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost > 3 } 
						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 3 } 
					}

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 0 } 
						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 2 } 
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = plane_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?raid_planes_lost]
					}

					hidden_effect = {
						raid_damage_units = {
							plane_loss = raid_planes_lostt
							ratio = no
						}
					}
				}
				
			}
			success = {
				victim_effects = {
					set_temp_variable_to_random = {
						var = missle_strike_dmg
						min = 40
						max = 80
						integer = yes
					}
					subtract_from_variable = {
						global.dnipro_obj_current_hp^10 = missle_strike_dmg
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost > 3 } 
						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 3 } 
					}

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 0 } 
						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 2 } 
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = plane_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?raid_planes_lost]
					}

					hidden_effect = {
						raid_damage_units = {
							plane_loss = raid_planes_lostt
							ratio = no
						}
					}
				}
			}
			success = {
				victim_effects = {
					set_temp_variable_to_random = {
						var = missle_strike_dmg
						min = 20
						max = 40
						integer = yes
					}
					subtract_from_variable = {
						global.dnipro_obj_current_hp^12 = missle_strike_dmg
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = bridges_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?missle_strike_dmg]
					}
				}
				actor_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lostt = 4 }
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 1 }

					var:target_state = {
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.aa_defense = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@anti_air_building }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.radar_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@radar_station }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.rocket_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@rocket_site }
					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { radar_mult = 0.5 }
					multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = radar_mult }
					multiply_temp_variable = { rocket_mult = radar_mult }

					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { check_variable = { rocket_mult = 0 } }
						}
						multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { aa_defense = 0 }
							}
							add_to_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }
						}
					}

					multiply_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = aa_defense integer = yes }

					clamp_temp_variable = {
						var = raid_planes_lost
						min = 0
					}

					round_temp_variable = raid_planes_lost

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost > 3 } 
						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 3 } 
					}

					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = plane_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?raid_planes_lost]
					}

					hidden_effect = {

							plane_loss = raid_planes_lostt
							ratio = no
						}
					}
				}
			}
			critical_success = {
				victim_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = {
						missle_strike_dmg = 50
					}
					subtract_from_variable = {
						global.dnipro_obj_current_hp^12 = missle_strike_dmg
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = bridges_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?missle_strike_dmg]
					}
				}
				actor_effects = {

					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 0 }

					var:target_state = {
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.aa_defense = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@anti_air_building }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.radar_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@radar_station }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.rocket_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@rocket_site }

					multiply_temp_variable = { rocket_mult = radar_mult }

					if = {

							NOT = { check_variable = { rocket_mult = 0 } }
						}

						if = {

							}
							add_to_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }

					multiply_temp_variable = { rocket_mult = radar_mult }

					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { check_variable = { rocket_mult = 0 } }
						}
						multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { aa_defense = 0 }
							}
							add_to_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }
						}
					}

					multiply_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = aa_defense integer = yes }

					clamp_temp_variable = {
						var = raid_planes_lost
						min = 0
					}

					round_temp_variable = raid_planes_lost

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost > 8 } 
						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 7 } 
					}

					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = plane_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?raid_planes_lost]
					}

					hidden_effect = {
						raid_damage_units = {
							plane_loss = raid_planes_lostt
							ratio = no
						}
					}
				}
				
			}
		}
	}

		}

				amount = { min = 4 }
			}
		}

		}

			types = {
				rocket_site
			}
		}
		success_factors = {
			success = {
				base = 0.4
				air_agility = {
					reference = 20
					weight = 0.1
					start_weight = -0.5
				}
				reliability = {
					reference = 1
					weight = 0.1
					start_weight = -0.1
				}

					reference = 1
					weight = 0.3
					start_weight = -0.100
				}

					reference = 1
					weight = -0.3
				}
				radar = {
					reference = 0
					weight = -0.2
				}
				interception = {
					reference = 5 
					weight = -0.2
				}
				intel = {
					weight = 0.1
					reference = 100
				}
			}
			disaster = {
				base = 0.2
			}
			critical = {
				base = 0.05
			}
		}
		success_levels = {
			failure = {
				victim_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = {
						missle_strike_dmg = 0
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = bridges_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?missle_strike_dmg]
					}
				}
				actor_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 4 }
					
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = plane_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?raid_planes_lost]
					}

					hidden_effect = {
						raid_damage_units = {
							plane_loss = raid_planes_lost
							ratio = no
						}
					}
				}
			}
			limited_success = {
				victim_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = {
						missle_strike_dmg = 20
					}
					subtract_from_variable = {
						global.dnipro_obj_current_hp^19 = missle_strike_dmg
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = bridges_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?missle_strike_dmg]
					}
				}
				actor_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lostt = 4 }
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 1 }

					var:target_state = {
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.aa_defense = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@anti_air_building }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.radar_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@radar_station }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.rocket_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@rocket_site }
					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { radar_mult = 0.5 }
					multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = radar_mult }
					multiply_temp_variable = { rocket_mult = radar_mult }

					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { check_variable = { rocket_mult = 0 } }
						}
						multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { aa_defense = 0 }
							}
							add_to_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }
						}
					}

					multiply_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = aa_defense integer = yes }

					clamp_temp_variable = {
						var = raid_planes_lost
						min = 0
					}

					round_temp_variable = raid_planes_lost

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost > 3 } 
						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 3 } 
					}

					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = bridges_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?missle_strike_dmg]
					}
				}
				actor_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 12 }
					
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = plane_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?raid_planes_lost]
					}

					hidden_effect = {
						raid_damage_units = {
							plane_loss = raid_planes_lost
							ratio = no
						}
					}
				}
			}
			limited_success = {
				victim_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = {
						missle_strike_dmg = 20
					}
					subtract_from_variable = {
						global.dnipro_obj_current_hp^19 = missle_strike_dmg
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = bridges_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?missle_strike_dmg]
					}
				}
				actor_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lostt = 12 }
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 1 }

					var:target_state = {
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.aa_defense = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@anti_air_building }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.radar_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@radar_station }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.rocket_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@rocket_site }
					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { radar_mult = 0.5 }
					multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = radar_mult }
					multiply_temp_variable = { rocket_mult = radar_mult }

					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { check_variable = { rocket_mult = 0 } }
						}
						multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { aa_defense = 0 }
							}
							add_to_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }
						}
					}

					multiply_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = aa_defense integer = yes }

					clamp_temp_variable = {
						var = raid_planes_lost
						min = 0
					}

					round_temp_variable = raid_planes_lost

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost > 12 } 
						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 10 } 
					}

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 0 } 
						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 4 } 
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = plane_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?raid_planes_lost]
					}

					hidden_effect = {
						raid_damage_units = {
							plane_loss = raid_planes_lostt
							ratio = no
						}
					}
				}
				
			}
			success = {
				victim_effects = {
					set_temp_variable_to_random = {
						var = missle_strike_dmg
						min = 20
						max = 40
						integer = yes
					}
					subtract_from_variable = {
						global.dnipro_obj_current_hp^19 = missle_strike_dmg
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = bridges_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?missle_strike_dmg]
					}
				}
				actor_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lostt = 12 }
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 1 }

					var:target_state = {
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.aa_defense = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@anti_air_building }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.radar_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@radar_station }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.rocket_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@rocket_site }
					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { radar_mult = 0.5 }
					multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = radar_mult }
					multiply_temp_variable = { rocket_mult = radar_mult }

					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { check_variable = { rocket_mult = 0 } }
						}
						multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { aa_defense = 0 }
							}
							add_to_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }
						}
					}

					multiply_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = aa_defense integer = yes }

					clamp_temp_variable = {
						var = raid_planes_lost
						min = 0
					}

					round_temp_variable = raid_planes_lost

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost > 10 } 
						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 8 } 
					}

					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = plane_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?raid_planes_lost]
					}

					hidden_effect = {
						raid_damage_units = {
							plane_loss = raid_planes_lostt
							ratio = no
						}
					}
				}
				
			}
			critical_success = {
				victim_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = {
						missle_strike_dmg = 50
					}
					subtract_from_variable = {
						global.dnipro_obj_current_hp^19 = missle_strike_dmg
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = bridges_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?missle_strike_dmg]
					}
				}
				actor_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lostt = 12 }
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 1 }

					var:target_state = {
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.aa_defense = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@anti_air_building }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.radar_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@radar_station }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.rocket_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@rocket_site }
					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { radar_mult = 0.5 }
					multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = radar_mult }
					multiply_temp_variable = { rocket_mult = radar_mult }

					if = {

							NOT = { check_variable = { rocket_mult = 0 } }
						}

						if = {

							}
							add_to_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }
						}
					}

						min = 0
					}

					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 1 }

					var:target_state = {
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.aa_defense = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@anti_air_building }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.radar_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@radar_station }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.rocket_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@rocket_site }
					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { radar_mult = 0.5 }
					multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = radar_mult }
					multiply_temp_variable = { rocket_mult = radar_mult }

					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { check_variable = { rocket_mult = 0 } }
						}
						multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { aa_defense = 0 }
							}
							add_to_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }
						}
					}

					multiply_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = aa_defense integer = yes }

					clamp_temp_variable = {
						var = raid_planes_lost
						min = 0
					}

					round_temp_variable = raid_planes_lost

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost > 3 } 
						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 3 } 
					}

					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = plane_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?raid_planes_lost]
					}

					hidden_effect = {
						raid_damage_units = {
							plane_loss = raid_planes_lostt
							ratio = no
						}
					}
				}
				
			}
			critical_success = {
				victim_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = {
						missle_strike_dmg = 100
					}
					subtract_from_variable = {
						global.dnipro_obj_current_hp^1 = missle_strike_dmg
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = bridges_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?missle_strike_dmg]
					}
				}
				actor_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lostt = 4 }
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 0 }

					var:target_state = {
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.aa_defense = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@anti_air_building }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.radar_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@radar_station }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.rocket_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@rocket_site }
					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { radar_mult = 0.5 }
					multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = radar_mult }
					multiply_temp_variable = { rocket_mult = radar_mult }

					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { check_variable = { rocket_mult = 0 } }
						}
						multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { aa_defense = 0 }
							}
							add_to_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }
						}
					}

					multiply_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = aa_defense integer = yes }

					clamp_temp_variable = {
						var = raid_planes_lost
						min = 0
					}

					round_temp_variable = raid_planes_lost

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost > 2 } 
						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 2 } 
					}

					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = plane_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?raid_planes_lost]
					}

					hidden_effect = {
						raid_damage_units = {
							plane_loss = raid_planes_lostt
							ratio = no
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

			}
		}

		}

			types = {
				rocket_site
			}
		}
		success_factors = {
			success = {
				base = 0.4
				air_agility = {
					reference = 20
					weight = 0.1
					start_weight = -0.5
				}
				reliability = {
					reference = 1
					weight = 0.1
					start_weight = -0.1
				}
				air_superiority = {
					reference = 1
					weight = 0.3

				}

					reference = 0

					reference = 5 
					weight = -0.2
				}

					weight = 0.1
					reference = 100
				}
			}
			disaster = {
				base = 0.2
			}
			critical = {
				base = 0.05
			}
		}
		success_levels = {
			failure = {
				victim_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = {
						missle_strike_dmg = 0
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = bridges_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?missle_strike_dmg]
					}
				}
				actor_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 4 }
					
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = plane_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?raid_planes_lost]
					}

					hidden_effect = {
						raid_damage_units = {
							plane_loss = raid_planes_lost
							ratio = no
						}
					}
				}
			}
			limited_success = {
				victim_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = {
						missle_strike_dmg = 40
					}
					subtract_from_variable = {
						global.dnipro_obj_current_hp^2 = missle_strike_dmg
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = bridges_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?missle_strike_dmg]
					}
				}
				actor_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lostt = 4 }
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 1 }

					var:target_state = {
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.aa_defense = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@anti_air_building }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.radar_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@radar_station }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.rocket_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@rocket_site }
					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { radar_mult = 0.5 }
					multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = radar_mult }
					multiply_temp_variable = { rocket_mult = radar_mult }

					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { check_variable = { rocket_mult = 0 } }
						}
						multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { aa_defense = 0 }
							}
							add_to_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }
						}
					}

					multiply_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = aa_defense integer = yes }

					clamp_temp_variable = {
						var = raid_planes_lost
						min = 0
					}

					round_temp_variable = raid_planes_lost

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost > 3 } 
						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 3 } 
					}

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 0 } 
						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 2 } 
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = plane_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?raid_planes_lost]
					}

					hidden_effect = {
						raid_damage_units = {
							plane_loss = raid_planes_lostt
							ratio = no
						}
					}
				}
				
			}
			success = {

						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.aa_defense = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@anti_air_building }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.radar_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@radar_station }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.rocket_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@rocket_site }
					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { radar_mult = 0.5 }
					multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = radar_mult }
					multiply_temp_variable = { rocket_mult = radar_mult }

					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { check_variable = { rocket_mult = 0 } }
						}
						multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { aa_defense = 0 }
							}
							add_to_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }
						}
					}

					multiply_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = aa_defense integer = yes }

					clamp_temp_variable = {
						var = raid_planes_lost
						min = 0
					}

					round_temp_variable = raid_planes_lost

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost > 3 } 
						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 3 } 
					}

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 0 } 
						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 2 } 
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = plane_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?raid_planes_lost]
					}

					hidden_effect = {
						raid_damage_units = {
							plane_loss = raid_planes_lostt
							ratio = no
						}
					}
				}
			}
			success = {
				victim_effects = {
					set_temp_variable_to_random = {
						var = missle_strike_dmg
						min = 20
						max = 40
						integer = yes
					}
					subtract_from_variable = {
						global.dnipro_obj_current_hp^3 = missle_strike_dmg
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = bridges_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?missle_strike_dmg]
					}
				}
				actor_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lostt = 4 }
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 1 }

					var:target_state = {
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.aa_defense = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@anti_air_building }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.radar_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@radar_station }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.rocket_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@rocket_site }
					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { radar_mult = 0.5 }
					multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = radar_mult }
					multiply_temp_variable = { rocket_mult = radar_mult }

					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { check_variable = { rocket_mult = 0 } }
						}
						multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { aa_defense = 0 }
							}
							add_to_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }
						}
					}

					multiply_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = aa_defense integer = yes }

					clamp_temp_variable = {
						var = raid_planes_lost
						min = 0
					}

					round_temp_variable = raid_planes_lost

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost > 3 } 
						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 3 } 
					}

					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = plane_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?raid_planes_lost]
					}

					hidden_effect = {
						raid_damage_units = {
							plane_loss = raid_planes_lostt
							ratio = no
						}
					}
				}
			}
			critical_success = {
				victim_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = {
						missle_strike_dmg = 50
					}
					subtract_from_variable = {
						global.dnipro_obj_current_hp^3 = missle_strike_dmg
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = bridges_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?missle_strike_dmg]
					}
				}
				actor_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lostt = 4 }
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 0 }

					var:target_state = {
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.aa_defense = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@anti_air_building }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.radar_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@radar_station }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.rocket_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@rocket_site }
					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { radar_mult = 0.5 }
					multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = radar_mult }
					multiply_temp_variable = { rocket_mult = radar_mult }

					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { check_variable = { rocket_mult = 0 } }
						}

						if = {

							}
							add_to_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }

					}

						}
					}
				}
				
			}
			critical_success = {
				victim_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = {
						missle_strike_dmg = 50
					}
					subtract_from_variable = {
						global.dnipro_obj_current_hp^3 = missle_strike_dmg
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = bridges_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?missle_strike_dmg]
					}
				}
				actor_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lostt = 12 }
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 1 }

					var:target_state = {
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.aa_defense = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@anti_air_building }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.radar_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@radar_station }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.rocket_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@rocket_site }
					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { radar_mult = 0.5 }
					multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = radar_mult }
					multiply_temp_variable = { rocket_mult = radar_mult }

					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { check_variable = { rocket_mult = 0 } }
						}
						multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { aa_defense = 0 }
							}
							add_to_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }
						}
					}

					multiply_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = aa_defense integer = yes }

					clamp_temp_variable = {
						var = raid_planes_lost
						min = 0
					}

					round_temp_variable = raid_planes_lost

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost > 8 } 
						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 7 } 
					}

					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = plane_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?raid_planes_lost]
					}

					hidden_effect = {
						raid_damage_units = {
							plane_loss = raid_planes_lostt
							ratio = no
						}
					}
				}
				
			}
		}

					weight = 0.1

					}

					reference = 20
					weight = 0.1
					start_weight = -0.5
				}
				reliability = {
					reference = 1
					weight = 0.1
					start_weight = -0.1
				}
				air_superiority = {
					reference = 1
					weight = 0.3
					start_weight = -0.100
				}

				anti_air = {
					reference = 1
					weight = -0.3
				}
				radar = {
					reference = 0
					weight = -0.2
				}
				interception = {
					reference = 5 
					weight = -0.2
				}
				intel = {
					weight = 0.1
					reference = 100
				}
			}
			disaster = {
				base = 0.2
			}
			critical = {
				base = 0.05
			}
		}
		success_levels = {
			failure = {
				victim_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = {
						missle_strike_dmg = 0
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = bridges_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?missle_strike_dmg]
					}
				}
				actor_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 12 }
					
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = plane_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?raid_planes_lost]
					}

					hidden_effect = {
						raid_damage_units = {
							plane_loss = raid_planes_lost
							ratio = no
						}
					}
				}
			}
			limited_success = {
				victim_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = {
						missle_strike_dmg = 20
					}
					subtract_from_variable = {
						global.dnipro_obj_current_hp^4 = missle_strike_dmg
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = bridges_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?missle_strike_dmg]
					}
				}
				actor_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lostt = 12 }
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 1 }

					var:target_state = {
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.aa_defense = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@anti_air_building }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.radar_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@radar_station }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.rocket_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@rocket_site }
					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { radar_mult = 0.5 }
					multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = radar_mult }
					multiply_temp_variable = { rocket_mult = radar_mult }

					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { check_variable = { rocket_mult = 0 } }
						}
						multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { aa_defense = 0 }
							}
							add_to_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }
						}
					}

					multiply_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = aa_defense integer = yes }

					clamp_temp_variable = {
						var = raid_planes_lost
						min = 0
					}

					round_temp_variable = raid_planes_lost

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost > 12 } 
						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 10 } 
					}

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 0 } 
						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 4 } 
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = plane_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?raid_planes_lost]
					}

					hidden_effect = {
						raid_damage_units = {
							plane_loss = raid_planes_lostt
							ratio = no
						}
					}
				}
				
			}
			success = {
				victim_effects = {
					set_temp_variable_to_random = {
						var = missle_strike_dmg
						min = 20
						max = 40
						integer = yes
					}
					subtract_from_variable = {
						global.dnipro_obj_current_hp^4 = missle_strike_dmg
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = bridges_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?missle_strike_dmg]
					}
				}
				actor_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lostt = 12 }
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 1 }

					var:target_state = {
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.aa_defense = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@anti_air_building }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.radar_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@radar_station }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.rocket_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@rocket_site }
					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { radar_mult = 0.5 }
					multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = radar_mult }
					multiply_temp_variable = { rocket_mult = radar_mult }

					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { check_variable = { rocket_mult = 0 } }
						}
						multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { aa_defense = 0 }
							}
							add_to_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }
						}
					}

					multiply_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = aa_defense integer = yes }

					clamp_temp_variable = {
						var = raid_planes_lost
						min = 0
					}

					round_temp_variable = raid_planes_lost

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost > 10 } 
						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 8 } 
					}

					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = plane_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?raid_planes_lost]
					}

					hidden_effect = {
						raid_damage_units = {
							plane_loss = raid_planes_lostt
							ratio = no
						}
					}
				}
				
			}
			critical_success = {
				victim_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = {
						missle_strike_dmg = 50
					}
					subtract_from_variable = {
						global.dnipro_obj_current_hp^4 = missle_strike_dmg
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = bridges_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?missle_strike_dmg]
					}
				}
				actor_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lostt = 12 }
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 1 }

					var:target_state = {
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.aa_defense = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@anti_air_building }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.radar_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@radar_station }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.rocket_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@rocket_site }
					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { radar_mult = 0.5 }
					multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = radar_mult }
					multiply_temp_variable = { rocket_mult = radar_mult }

							plane_loss = raid_planes_lostt
							ratio = no
						}
					}
				}
				
			}
			success = {
				victim_effects = {
					set_temp_variable_to_random = {
						var = missle_strike_dmg
						min = 40
						max = 80
						integer = yes
					}
					subtract_from_variable = {
						global.dnipro_obj_current_hp^5 = missle_strike_dmg
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = bridges_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?missle_strike_dmg]
					}
				}
				actor_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lostt = 4 }
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 1 }

					var:target_state = {
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.aa_defense = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@anti_air_building }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.radar_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@radar_station }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.rocket_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@rocket_site }
					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { radar_mult = 0.5 }
					multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = radar_mult }
					multiply_temp_variable = { rocket_mult = radar_mult }

					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { check_variable = { rocket_mult = 0 } }
						}
						multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { aa_defense = 0 }
							}
							add_to_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }
						}
					}

					multiply_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = aa_defense integer = yes }

					clamp_temp_variable = {
						var = raid_planes_lost
						min = 0
					}

					round_temp_variable = raid_planes_lost

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost > 3 } 
						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 3 } 
					}

					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = plane_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?raid_planes_lost]
					}

					hidden_effect = {
						raid_damage_units = {
							plane_loss = raid_planes_lostt
							ratio = no
						}
					}
				}
				
			}
			critical_success = {
				victim_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = {
						missle_strike_dmg = 100
					}
					subtract_from_variable = {
						global.dnipro_obj_current_hp^5 = missle_strike_dmg
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = bridges_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?missle_strike_dmg]
					}
				}
				actor_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lostt = 4 }
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 0 }

					var:target_state = {
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.aa_defense = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@anti_air_building }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.radar_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@radar_station }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.rocket_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@rocket_site }
					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { radar_mult = 0.5 }
					multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = radar_mult }
					multiply_temp_variable = { rocket_mult = radar_mult }

					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { check_variable = { rocket_mult = 0 } }
						}
						multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { aa_defense = 0 }
							}
							add_to_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }
						}
					}

					clamp_temp_variable = {

						min = 0

							}
							add_to_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }
						}
					}

					multiply_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = aa_defense integer = yes }

					clamp_temp_variable = {
						var = raid_planes_lost
						min = 0
					}

					round_temp_variable = raid_planes_lost

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost > 2 } 
						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 2 } 
					}

					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = plane_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?raid_planes_lost]
					}

					hidden_effect = {
						raid_damage_units = {
							plane_loss = raid_planes_lostt
							ratio = no
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

				base = 0.05
			}

		success_levels = {
			failure = {
				victim_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = {
						missle_strike_dmg = 0
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = bridges_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?missle_strike_dmg]
					}
				}
				actor_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 4 }

						localization_key = plane_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?raid_planes_lost]
					}

					hidden_effect = {

							plane_loss = raid_planes_lost
							ratio = no
						}
					}
				}
			}
			limited_success = {
				victim_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = {
						missle_strike_dmg = 40
					}
					subtract_from_variable = {
						global.dnipro_obj_current_hp^6 = missle_strike_dmg
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = bridges_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?missle_strike_dmg]
					}
				}
				actor_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lostt = 4 }
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 1 }

					var:target_state = {
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.aa_defense = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@anti_air_building }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.radar_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@radar_station }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.rocket_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@rocket_site }
					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { radar_mult = 0.5 }
					multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = radar_mult }
					multiply_temp_variable = { rocket_mult = radar_mult }

					if = {

							NOT = { check_variable = { rocket_mult = 0 } }
						}
						multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { aa_defense = 0 }
							}
							add_to_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }
						}
					}

					clamp_temp_variable = {
						var = raid_planes_lost
						min = 0
					}

					round_temp_variable = raid_planes_lost

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost > 3 } 
						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 3 } 
					}

						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.radar_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@radar_station }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.rocket_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@rocket_site }
					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { radar_mult = 0.5 }
					multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = radar_mult }
					multiply_temp_variable = { rocket_mult = radar_mult }

					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { check_variable = { rocket_mult = 0 } }
						}
						multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { aa_defense = 0 }
							}
							add_to_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }
						}
					}

					multiply_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = aa_defense integer = yes }

					clamp_temp_variable = {
						var = raid_planes_lost
						min = 0
					}

					round_temp_variable = raid_planes_lost

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost > 3 } 
						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 3 } 
					}

					if = { 
						limit = {

								check_variable = { aa_defense = 0 }
							}
							add_to_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }
						}
					}

					multiply_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = aa_defense integer = yes }

					clamp_temp_variable = {
						var = raid_planes_lost
						min = 0
					}

					round_temp_variable = raid_planes_lost

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost > 10 } 
						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 8 } 
					}

					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = plane_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?raid_planes_lost]
					}

					hidden_effect = {
						raid_damage_units = {
							plane_loss = raid_planes_lostt
							ratio = no
						}
					}
				}
				
			}
			critical_success = {
				victim_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = {
						missle_strike_dmg = 50
					}
					subtract_from_variable = {
						global.dnipro_obj_current_hp^7 = missle_strike_dmg
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = bridges_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?missle_strike_dmg]
					}
				}
				actor_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lostt = 12 }
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 1 }

					var:target_state = {
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.aa_defense = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@anti_air_building }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.radar_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@radar_station }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.rocket_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@rocket_site }
					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { radar_mult = 0.5 }
					multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = radar_mult }
					multiply_temp_variable = { rocket_mult = radar_mult }

					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { check_variable = { rocket_mult = 0 } }
						}
						multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { aa_defense = 0 }
							}
							add_to_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }
						}
					}

					multiply_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = aa_defense integer = yes }

					clamp_temp_variable = {
						var = raid_planes_lost
						min = 0
					}

					round_temp_variable = raid_planes_lost

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost > 8 } 
						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 7 } 
					}

					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = plane_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?raid_planes_lost]
					}

					hidden_effect = {
						raid_damage_units = {
							plane_loss = raid_planes_lostt
							ratio = no
						}
					}
				}
				
			}
		}

				amount = { min = 4 }
			}
		}

		}

				rocket_site
			}
		}
		success_factors = {

					reference = 20
					weight = 0.1
					start_weight = -0.5
				}

					reference = 1
					weight = 0.1
					start_weight = -0.1
				}

					reference = 1
					weight = 0.3
					start_weight = -0.100
				}

					reference = 1
					weight = -0.3
				}

					reference = 0
					weight = -0.2
				}
				interception = {
					reference = 5 
					weight = -0.2
				}
				intel = {
					weight = 0.1
					reference = 100
				}
			}
			disaster = {
				base = 0.2
			}
			critical = {
				base = 0.05
			}
		}
		success_levels = {
			failure = {
				victim_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = {
						missle_strike_dmg = 0

				}

							ratio = no
						}
					}
				}
			}

					}
					subtract_from_variable = {

					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = bridges_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?missle_strike_dmg]
					}
				}
				actor_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lostt = 4 }
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 1 }

					var:target_state = {

						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.radar_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@radar_station }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.rocket_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@rocket_site }
					}

			has_war_with = FROM
		}
		target_type = {
			province = 6558
		}
		target_icon = GFX_other_target_icon
		launch_sound = raid_launch_air
		arrow = {
			type = air
		}
		unit_model = {
		}
		unit_requirements = {
			equipment = {
				type = { ukr_drone_missile_equipment nto_guided_uav_equipment ukr_guided_uav_equipment rus_guided_uav_equipment }
				amount = { min = 12 }
			}
		}
		additional_equipment = {
		}
		starting_point = {
			types = {
				rocket_site
			}
		}
		success_factors = {
			success = {
				base = 0.4
				air_agility = {
					reference = 20
					weight = 0.1
					start_weight = -0.5
				}
				reliability = {
					reference = 1
					weight = 0.1
					start_weight = -0.1
				}
				air_superiority = {
					reference = 1
					weight = 0.3
					start_weight = -0.100
				}

				anti_air = {
					reference = 1
					weight = -0.3
				}
				radar = {
					reference = 0
					weight = -0.2
				}
				interception = {
					reference = 5 
					weight = -0.2
				}
				intel = {
					weight = 0.1
					reference = 100
				}
			}
			disaster = {
				base = 0.2
			}
			critical = {
				base = 0.05
			}
		}
		success_levels = {
			failure = {
				victim_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = {
						missle_strike_dmg = 0
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = bridges_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?missle_strike_dmg]
					}
				}
				actor_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 12 }
					
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = plane_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?raid_planes_lost]
					}

					hidden_effect = {
						raid_damage_units = {
							plane_loss = raid_planes_lostt
							ratio = no
						}
					}
				}
			}
			limited_success = {
				victim_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = {
						missle_strike_dmg = 20
					}
					subtract_from_variable = {
						global.dnipro_obj_current_hp^9 = missle_strike_dmg
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = bridges_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?missle_strike_dmg]
					}
				}
				actor_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lostt = 12 }
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 1 }

					var:target_state = {
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.aa_defense = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@anti_air_building }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.radar_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@radar_station }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.rocket_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@rocket_site }
					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { radar_mult = 0.5 }
					multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = radar_mult }
					multiply_temp_variable = { rocket_mult = radar_mult }

					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { check_variable = { rocket_mult = 0 } }
						}
						multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { aa_defense = 0 }
							}
							add_to_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }
						}
					}

					multiply_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = aa_defense integer = yes }

					clamp_temp_variable = {
						var = raid_planes_lost
						min = 0
					}

					round_temp_variable = raid_planes_lost

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost > 12 } 
						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 10 } 
					}

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 0 } 
						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 4 } 
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = plane_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?raid_planes_lost]
					}

					hidden_effect = {
						raid_damage_units = {
							plane_loss = raid_planes_lostt
							ratio = no
						}
					}
				}
				
			}
			success = {
				victim_effects = {
					set_temp_variable_to_random = {
						var = missle_strike_dmg
						min = 20
						max = 40
						integer = yes
					}
					subtract_from_variable = {
						global.dnipro_obj_current_hp^9 = missle_strike_dmg
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = bridges_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?missle_strike_dmg]
					}
				}
				actor_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lostt = 12 }
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 1 }

					var:target_state = {
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.aa_defense = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@anti_air_building }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.radar_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@radar_station }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.rocket_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@rocket_site }
					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { radar_mult = 0.5 }
					multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = radar_mult }
					multiply_temp_variable = { rocket_mult = radar_mult }

					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { check_variable = { rocket_mult = 0 } }
						}
						multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { aa_defense = 0 }
							}
							add_to_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }
						}
					}

					multiply_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = aa_defense integer = yes }

					clamp_temp_variable = {
						var = raid_planes_lost
						min = 0
					}

					round_temp_variable = raid_planes_lost

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost > 10 } 
						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 8 } 
					}

					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = plane_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?raid_planes_lost]
					}

					hidden_effect = {
						raid_damage_units = {
							plane_loss = raid_planes_lostt
							ratio = no
						}
					}
				}
				
			}
			critical_success = {
				victim_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = {
						missle_strike_dmg = 50
					}
					subtract_from_variable = {
						global.dnipro_obj_current_hp^9 = missle_strike_dmg
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {

					}
				}
				actor_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lostt = 12 }
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 1 }

					var:target_state = {
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.aa_defense = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@anti_air_building }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.radar_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@radar_station }

					}

					multiply_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = aa_defense integer = yes }

					clamp_temp_variable = {
						var = raid_planes_lost
						min = 0
					}

					round_temp_variable = raid_planes_lost

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost > 3 } 
						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 3 } 
					}

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 0 }

					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 0 }

					var:target_state = {
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.aa_defense = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@anti_air_building }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.radar_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@radar_station }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.rocket_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@rocket_site }
					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { radar_mult = 0.5 }
					multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = radar_mult }
					multiply_temp_variable = { rocket_mult = radar_mult }

					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { check_variable = { rocket_mult = 0 } }
						}
						multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { aa_defense = 0 }
							}
							add_to_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }
						}
					}

					multiply_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = aa_defense integer = yes }

					clamp_temp_variable = {
						var = raid_planes_lost
						min = 0
					}

					round_temp_variable = raid_planes_lost

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost > 2 } 
						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 2 } 
					}

					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = plane_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?raid_planes_lost]
					}

					hidden_effect = {
						raid_damage_units = {
							plane_loss = raid_planes_lostt
							ratio = no
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

					var:target_state = {
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.aa_defense = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@anti_air_building }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.radar_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@radar_station }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.rocket_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@rocket_site }
					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { radar_mult = 0.5 }
					multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = radar_mult }
					multiply_temp_variable = { rocket_mult = radar_mult }

					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { check_variable = { rocket_mult = 0 } }
						}
						multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { aa_defense = 0 }
							}
							add_to_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }
						}
					}

					multiply_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = aa_defense integer = yes }

					clamp_temp_variable = {
						var = raid_planes_lost
						min = 0
					}

					round_temp_variable = raid_planes_lost

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost > 3 } 
						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 3 } 
					}

					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lostt = 12 }
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 1 }

					var:target_state = {
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.aa_defense = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@anti_air_building }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.radar_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@radar_station }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.rocket_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@rocket_site }
					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { radar_mult = 0.5 }
					multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = radar_mult }
					multiply_temp_variable = { rocket_mult = radar_mult }

					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { check_variable = { rocket_mult = 0 } }
						}
						multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { aa_defense = 0 }
							}
							add_to_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }
						}
					}

					multiply_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = aa_defense integer = yes }

					clamp_temp_variable = {
						var = raid_planes_lost
						min = 0
					}

					round_temp_variable = raid_planes_lost

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost > 10 } 
						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 8 } 
					}

					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = plane_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?raid_planes_lost]
					}

					hidden_effect = {
						raid_damage_units = {
							plane_loss = raid_planes_lostt
							ratio = no
						}
					}
				}
				
			}
			critical_success = {
				victim_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = {
						missle_strike_dmg = 50
					}
					subtract_from_variable = {
						global.dnipro_obj_current_hp^14 = missle_strike_dmg
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = bridges_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?missle_strike_dmg]
					}
				}
				actor_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lostt = 12 }
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 1 }

					var:target_state = {
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.aa_defense = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@anti_air_building }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.radar_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@radar_station }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.rocket_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@rocket_site }
					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { radar_mult = 0.5 }
					multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = radar_mult }
					multiply_temp_variable = { rocket_mult = radar_mult }

					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { check_variable = { rocket_mult = 0 } }
						}
						multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { aa_defense = 0 }
							}
							add_to_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }
						}
					}

					multiply_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = aa_defense integer = yes }

					clamp_temp_variable = {

						min = 0

	rus_strikes_on_bridges_DNIPRO_AMUR_STRAIT_drone = {
		days_to_prepare = 1
		days_re_enable = 0
		category = on_bridge_strikes
		command_power = 0
		 ai_will_do = {
		 	base = 1.0
		 	modifier = {
		 		factor = 5.0
		 		date > 2022.3.1
		 	}
		 	modifier = {
		 		factor = 0.2
		 		date < 2022.3.1
		 	}
		 }
		allowed = {
			has_dlc = "Gotterdammerung"
		}
		visible = {
		}
		show_target = {
			NOT = { is_in_faction_with = FROM }
			has_war_with = FROM
		}
		available = {
			has_war_with = FROM
		}
		target_type = {
			province = 18751
		}
		target_icon = GFX_other_target_icon
		launch_sound = raid_launch_air
		arrow = {
			type = air
		}
		unit_model = {
		}
		unit_requirements = {
			equipment = {
				type = { ukr_drone_missile_equipment nto_guided_uav_equipment ukr_guided_uav_equipment rus_guided_uav_equipment }
				amount = { min = 12 }
			}
		}
		additional_equipment = {
		}
		starting_point = {
			types = {
				rocket_site
			}
		}
		success_factors = {
			success = {
				base = 0.4
				air_agility = {
					reference = 20
					weight = 0.1
					start_weight = -0.5
				}
				reliability = {
					reference = 1
					weight = 0.1
					start_weight = -0.1
				}
				air_superiority = {
					reference = 1
					weight = 0.3
					start_weight = -0.100
				}

				anti_air = {
					reference = 1
					weight = -0.3
				}
				radar = {
					reference = 0
					weight = -0.2
				}
				interception = {
					reference = 5 
					weight = -0.2
				}
				intel = {
					weight = 0.1
					reference = 100
				}
			}
			disaster = {
				base = 0.2
			}
			critical = {
				base = 0.05
			}
		}
		success_levels = {
			failure = {
				victim_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = {
						missle_strike_dmg = 0
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = bridges_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?missle_strike_dmg]
					}
				}
				actor_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 12 }
					
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = plane_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?raid_planes_lost]
					}

					hidden_effect = {
						raid_damage_units = {
							plane_loss = raid_planes_lostt
							ratio = no
						}
					}
				}
			}
			limited_success = {
				victim_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = {
						missle_strike_dmg = 20
					}
					subtract_from_variable = {
						global.dnipro_obj_current_hp^15 = missle_strike_dmg
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = bridges_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?missle_strike_dmg]
					}
				}
				actor_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lostt = 12 }
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 1 }

					var:target_state = {
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.aa_defense = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@anti_air_building }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.radar_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@radar_station }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.rocket_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@rocket_site }
					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { radar_mult = 0.5 }
					multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = radar_mult }
					multiply_temp_variable = { rocket_mult = radar_mult }

					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { check_variable = { rocket_mult = 0 } }
						}
						multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { aa_defense = 0 }
							}
							add_to_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }
						}
					}

					multiply_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = aa_defense integer = yes }

					clamp_temp_variable = {
						var = raid_planes_lost
						min = 0
					}

					round_temp_variable = raid_planes_lost

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost > 12 } 
						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 10 } 
					}

					if = { 
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 0 } 
						} 
						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 4 } 
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = plane_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?raid_planes_lost]
					}

					hidden_effect = {
						raid_damage_units = {
							plane_loss = raid_planes_lostt
							ratio = no
						}
					}
				}
				
			}
			success = {
				victim_effects = {
					set_temp_variable_to_random = {
						var = missle_strike_dmg
						min = 20
						max = 40
						integer = yes
					}
					subtract_from_variable = {
						global.dnipro_obj_current_hp^15 = missle_strike_dmg
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = {
						localization_key = bridges_raid_losses_tt
						LOSSES = [?missle_strike_dmg]
					}
				}
				actor_effects = {
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lostt = 12 }
					set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 1 }

					var:target_state = {

						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.radar_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@radar_station }
						set_temp_variable = { ROOT.rocket_mult = THIS.non_damaged_building_level@rocket_site }
					}

					add_to_temp_variable = { radar_mult = 0.5 }
					multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = radar_mult }
					multiply_temp_variable = { rocket_mult = radar_mult }

					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { check_variable = { rocket_mult = 0 } }
						}
						multiply_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { aa_defense = 0 }
							}
							add_to_temp_variable = { aa_defense = rocket_mult }
						}
					}

					multiply_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = aa_defense integer = yes }

					clamp_temp_variable = {
						var = raid_planes_lost

					round_temp_variable = raid_planes_lost

						set_temp_variable = { raid_planes_lost = 8 }

					custom_effect_tooltip = {
